__typename?: 'Query';
  account?: Maybe<Account>;
  activityPaginated?: Maybe<ActivityPaginated>;
  /** @deprecated Use place instead */
  address?: Maybe<AddressInfo>;
  availablePushNotificationTypes: Array<PushNotificationTypeDetails>;
  /**
   * Returns a non nullable list of nullable bookmarkable union types.
   * The order of these bookmarks align with the `items` input given.
   * If an element of the `codes` is malformed, the index of the
   * response will be null and can be ignored.
   *
   * The type prefix should align with a GraphQL type, the ID and the
   * tenant slug. This query can only support one tenant at a time.
   * If `codes` contains bookmarks across multiple tenants it will
   * be treated as a bad request. If the tenant header is provided,
   * and the input entries do not define their own `tenant` field,
   * the tenant defined in the header will implicitly be used.
   *
   * When profile bookmark inputs are provided, it is possible that
   * the `DiscoverProfile` response will return `null`. This indicates
   * that the profile has been marked as private. It is also possible
   * for a different profile to be returned when the bookmarked profile
   * was claimed. This can be confirmed by comparing the ID provided
   * with the bookmark versus the one that was returned as part of the
   * response.
   *
   * The response will only respond with 50 bookmarkable entities. Any
   * attempt to provide more than 50 codes is treated as a bad request.
   */
  bookmarks?: Maybe<Array<Maybe<Bookmarkable>>>;
  configuration: Configuration;
  /**
   * Returns the dependent's profile details. Users must be authenticated
   * to use this query and the ID provided must be a valid dependent that
   * the account holder supervises.
   */
  dependantProfile?: Maybe<Profile>;
  discoverCompetitions: Array<DiscoverCompetition>;
  discoverDiscount?: Maybe<Discount>;
  discoverFixtureByDate: DiscoverDateFixture;
  discoverFixtureByRound: DiscoverRoundFixture;
  discoverGame?: Maybe<DiscoverGame>;
  discoverGrade?: Maybe<DiscoverGrade>;
  discoverGradeFixture: Array<DiscoverRound>;
  discoverMilestone?: Maybe<DiscoverMilestone>;
  /**
   * Return a milestones for a profile given a list of game counts.
   * Limit field is optional and will return the highest milestones with maximum limit count.
   */
  discoverMilestones?: Maybe<Array<DiscoverMilestone>>;
  discoverOrganisation?: Maybe<DiscoverOrganisation>;
  discoverOrganisationPosts?: Maybe<DiscoverOrganisationPosts>;
  discoverOrganisations: DiscoverOrganisationResults;
  discoverPost?: Maybe<DiscoverPost>;
  discoverSeason?: Maybe<DiscoverSeason>;
  discoverSeasonRegistration: DiscoverRegistration;
  discoverSocialTeamRegistration: DiscoverSocialTeamRegistration;
  discoverTeam?: Maybe<DiscoverTeam>;
  discoverTeamFixture: Array<DiscoverRound>;
  discoverTeams: Array<DiscoverTeam>;
  /**
   * Find profiles that would be classed as duplicates based of user
   * submitted information. This is primarily used to find dependants
   * that exist in our systems, but have changed their details that the
   * existing criteria defined in the `Profile.duplicateProfiles` no longer
   * works. Dependant searches are scoped by the authenticated user;
   * that is that the authenticated user making the query _must_ be
   * the account holder.
   *
   * Users must be authenticated to make this GraphQL mutation.
   */
  duplicateProfiles?: Maybe<Array<DuplicateProfile>>;
  gameSheetDownload?: Maybe<GameSheetDownloadResponse>;
  /** Return the award configuration, votes and player lineup for a team in a game */
  gameTeamAward?: Maybe<GameTeamAwardResponse>;
  /**
   * Validate if the provided lineup is valid.
   *
   * This is currently used when adding additional players to a lineup.
   */
  gameTeamLineupValidate?: Maybe<Array<GameTeamLineupValidateResult>>;
  /** Get statistics for a given grade based on given sorting and pagination parameters */
  gradePlayerStatistics?: Maybe<GradePlayerStatistics>;
  /** Get list of teams from grade statistics for a given grade */
  gradePlayerStatisticsTeamList?: Maybe<Array<StatisticsTeam>>;
  /** Get an incident by ID */
  incident?: Maybe<Incident>;
  invoiceList: InvoiceList;
  /**
   * Get the game availability for all participants related to the logged in profile
   * @deprecated use myProfilesGameAvailability instead
   */
  myPlayersGameAvailability?: Maybe<MyPlayersGameAvailabilityResponse>;
  /** Get the game availability for all profiles related to the logged in account */
  myProfilesGameAvailability?: Maybe<MyProfilesGameAvailabilityResponse>;
  myTeamsGame?: Maybe<MyTeamsGame>;
  myTeamsGamePaymentRequest?: Maybe<MyTeamsGamePaymentRequestResponse>;
  /** Get a list of participants in an organisation and season */
  myTeamsParticipants?: Maybe<MyTeamsParticipantList>;
  myTeamsTeam?: Maybe<MyTeamsTeam>;
  /** Placeholder query with null response that is used as a template for queries that are not implemented yet */
  nullResponse?: Maybe<NullResponse>;
  organisationRegistrations: Array<DiscoverRegistration>;
  participant: Participant;
  /** Get a payment request product by its ID */
  paymentRequestProduct?: Maybe<Product>;
  place?: Maybe<AddressInfo>;
  /**
   * Returns the authenticated user's profile details. The ID argument is
   * never referred to in the server implementation. This exists only to
   * ensure that this change is a non-breaking.
   */
  profile?: Maybe<Profile>;
  profilePhotoVerificationUploadURL: SignedUrl;
  profileSearch?: Maybe<ProfileSearchResult>;
  profileTenantHistory: ProfileTenantDetails;
  publicProfile?: Maybe<DiscoverProfile>;
  publicProfileStatistics?: Maybe<PublicProfileStatistics>;
  /**
   * Get a list of teams for a given profile allocated as a player.
   * The max number of teams per profile has been capped to 50 teams.
   * Returns null if:
   * 1. Profile is not visible
   */
  publicProfileTeams?: Maybe<Array<DiscoverTeam>>;
  pushNotificationSettings: PushNotificationUserSettings;
  /**
   * The query allows asserting the registration related input by running all required policies and
   * return a hash key that will be used to submit the order, the hash key will be valid for a limited time
   * and needs to be used by the order submit mutation.
   */
  registrationAssert: AssertHash;
  registrationCheck?: Maybe<RegistrationCheckResult>;
  registrationSettings?: Maybe<RegistrationSettings>;
  /** @deprecated Use searchPlaces instead */
  searchAddresses: Array<Scalars['String']>;
  searchPlaces: Array<PlacesAutocomplete>;
  seasonRegistrationCart: CartPayload;
  seasonRegistrations: Array<DiscoverRegistration>;
  /** Get a shop cart for a given ID */
  shopCart?: Maybe<ShopCart>;
  /**
   * Get a product by its ID
   * organisation code parameter has been added later to support easy merch products retrieval
   * hence to avoid breaking changes, it is optional
   */
  shopProduct?: Maybe<Product>;
  /**
   * Get a list of products available/visible in the shop for a given organisation
   * The result is a shallow products list, excluding the product variants and custom fields
   */
  shopProducts?: Maybe<Array<ShallowProduct>>;
  socialTeamRegistration?: Maybe<SocialTeamRegistration>;
  socialTeamRegistrationCart: CartPayload;
  sponsorBanner: SponsorBanner;
  tenantConfiguration?: Maybe<TenantConfiguration>;
  /**
   * Finds upcoming team events for a set of bookmarks. These bookmarks must all be teams,
   * all other bookmark types will be ignored. While a majority of these team events will
   * be games, they also represent byes and scenarios where the team may not have been
   * allocated.
   *
   * See the UpcomingTeamEventTimeline documentation regarding the contents of the timeline.
   *
   * A tenant header must be provided.
   */
  upcomingTeamEvents?: Maybe<UpcomingTeamEventTimeline>;
  /**
   * Finds team events for a set of bookmarks from a specific start date. These bookmarks
   * must all be teams, all other bookmark types will be ignored.
   * If the number of events exceed the limit of the response, it will cut off on a specific
   * date which is available as the lastDate field, and the hasMoreAfterLastDate flag will be
   * TRUE. Pagination is based on dates, and not any exact number of events.
   */
  upcomingTeamEventsPaginated?: Maybe<UpcomingTeamEventsPaginated>;

__typename?: 'Profile';
  /** Accreditations, training certifications and their completion status */
  accreditations?: Maybe<Array<ProfileAccreditation>>;
  address?: Maybe<Address>;
  childSafety?: Maybe<Array<FieldSet>>;
  childSafetyChecks?: Maybe<Array<ProfileChildSafetyCheck>>;
  coachingAccreditation?: Maybe<CoachingAccreditation>;
  concussionIncidents?: Maybe<Array<Incident>>;
  countryOfBirth?: Maybe<Scalars['String']>;
  dateOfBirth?: Maybe<Scalars['ISODate']>;
  dependants?: Maybe<Array<Profile>>;
  disabilities?: Maybe<Array<TenantField>>;
  /** @deprecated use hasDisability and disabilities */
  disability?: Maybe<TenantField>;
  disabilityHelp?: Maybe<Scalars['String']>;
  /**
   * Returns a list of profiles that are possible duplicates of this one.
   * The matching criteria is as follows:
   *
   * - The last name MUST be an exact match
   * - The first name MUST be an exact match OR be an alternative name
   * - The gender MUST be an exact match
   * - The date of birth MUST be an exact match
   *
   * > Alternative names are commonly known aliases for a given name. For example,
   * > `Catherine` can be an alias to `Cat`.
   *
   * This can be used in two different flows; in a registration or direct
   * flow. Registration flows should provide the `registrationCode` argument
   * which is used to verify whether duplicate profiles have existing registrations
   * with the organisation for given registration.
   *
   * For example, if `registrationCode` `alice` is provided and is organised by
   * organisation `bob`, then duplicate profiles must have a previous registration
   * with organisation `bob`.
   *
   * Direct flows can provide a first name, last name, gender and/or a date of birth.
   * Direct flows are used outside an registration context and the `registrationCode`
   * should not be supplied in these circumstances. When these are supplied, these
   * values are used to as part of the matching criteria instead.
   *
   * A request that mixes these arguments would result in a bad request.
   *
   * Use the `Query.duplicateProfiles` for direct flows.
   */
  duplicateProfiles?: Maybe<Array<DuplicateProfile>>;
  email?: Maybe<Scalars['String']>;
  emergencyContact?: Maybe<EmergencyContact>;
  /**
   * Used to store links to external accounts
   * For example, it can store the link to someones Cricket ID account
   */
  externalAccounts: Array<ExternalAccount>;
  firstName: Scalars['String'];
  gender?: Maybe<TenantField>;
  genderSelfDescribe?: Maybe<Scalars['String']>;
  guardian1CountryOfBirth?: Maybe<Scalars['String']>;
  guardian2CountryOfBirth?: Maybe<Scalars['String']>;
  guardianBornOverseas?: Maybe<TenantField>;
  guardians?: Maybe<Array<PossibleGuardian>>;
  hasDisability?: Maybe<TenantField>;
  homeNumber?: Maybe<Scalars['String']>;
  id: Scalars['ID'];
  identityVerificationRequired?: Maybe<Scalars['Boolean']>;
  identityVerifications?: Maybe<Array<IdentityVerification>>;
  indigenousDescent?: Maybe<TenantField>;
  /**
   * Resolves to the last known interacted organisations that the profile is associated with.
   * This interaction is determined by their tenant. For example, this could reflect the
   * organisation associated with the profile's last known registration and/or their latest
   * club affiliation.
   */
  lastInteractedOrganisations?: Maybe<Array<DiscoverOrganisation>>;
  lastName: Scalars['String'];
  /** Endurance zone membership reward url */
  membershipRewardUrl?: Maybe<Scalars['String']>;
  memberships: Array<Membership>;
  migratedEmail?: Maybe<Scalars['String']>;
  migrationID?: Maybe<Scalars['String']>;
  mobileNumber?: Maybe<Mobile>;
  /**
   * List of teams that the profile has participated in. Can be filtered by
   * season status (e.g. to hide teams in completed seasons)
   */
  myTeamsList?: Maybe<MyTeamsList>;
  nationalityVerifications: Array<NationalityVerification>;
  otherDisability?: Maybe<Scalars['String']>;
  /** The signed URL which points to photo to verify the identity of a person IRL. */
  photoVerificationURL?: Maybe<Scalars['String']>;
  preferredName?: Maybe<Scalars['String']>;
  profilePhotoVerificationURL?: Maybe<SignedUrl>;
  profileQuestions?: Maybe<Array<FieldSet>>;
  registrationHistory?: Maybe<Array<RegistrationHistory>>;
  socialTeams: Array<TeamOrigin>;
  transferRequests: Array<TransferRequest>;
  videoConsent?: Maybe<Scalars['Boolean']>;
  visaClassifications: Array<VisaClassification>;
  visible: Scalars['Boolean'];
  wwc?: Maybe<Wwc>;

   * returned based on whether they are an event statistic or a total statistic.

  /**
   * This will be true if the player has a season permit. We don't return the season permit dates,
   * as we assume that if the FillInPlayer was added to the lineup, their season permit must be valid on the game date

__typename?: 'PlayerPeriod';
  /**
   * Array of positions the player had during the current period (if in-game
   * positions is enabled). NOTE: this only tracks each unique position, ordered by
   * the tenant-config positions sort-order. For example, if a player in netball
   * was on the interchange, subbed into center, then changed to goal attack, this
   * would be returned as ["GA", "C", "INT"]
   */
  inGamePositions?: Maybe<Array<GamePlayerPosition>>;
  /**
   * If the game is in overtime, this will always start from 1 (even if there is
   * only 1 overtime period in the game).
   */
  overtimeSequenceNo?: Maybe<Scalars['Int']>;
  period?: Maybe<Period>;

  /** @deprecated field not used anymore */

  /**
   * PeriodValue along with Side determines the innings the player period stats were applied to.
   * For Eg: In Cricket,
   * A Player can have stats in both FIRST_INNINGS
   * If he bats in his team's FIRST_INNINGS and bowls in the other team's FIRST_INNINGS.
   * side property determines which period to apply the statistics on the graph.
   * side applicable to innings based games
   */

  statistics?: Maybe<Array<Statistic>>;
  status?: Maybe<PlayerPeriodStatusValue>;
  type?: Maybe<PeriodType>;

   * process.

   * shop. Defaults to `false` when not provided.

   * Categories associated with the product. For example, a shirt product
   * may have the 'Size' and 'Colour' categories.
   */

   * Custom fields associated with the product and attribute options.
   * Empty if no custom fields associated with the product or attribute options.

   * @deprecated use registrationSettings
   */

  name: Scalars['String'];
  productType: ProductType;
  /**
   * Since the product type is now used by both registration and shop, this field would only contain
   * the registration related settings for the product. Thus the product type can be used by both
   * registration and shop.
   */
  registrationSettings?: Maybe<ProductRegistrationSettings>;
  /** @deprecated use registrationSettings */
  required?: Maybe<Scalars['Boolean']>;
  /** Generic property to display any product related metadata such validFrom or validTo */
  settings?: Maybe<ProductSettings>;
  variants: Array<ProductVariant>;
};

/**
 * An attribute/category that belongs to a given product. For example,
 * 'Size' is a valid category/attribute for a product to have.
 */

   * this could be options such as 'Small', 'Medium', 'Large'.

   * The tenants name details. The `name` subfield is the human readable name
   * and should be displayed to the user, while the `value` is the computed
   * name, mainly used for scoping. Requests that require such scoping should
   * provide it in the header when the request is made.
   */
  tenants: Array<TenantField>;
  /**
   * The list of tenant slugs. The `name` field is a short name of the tenant
   * while value is a tenant slug. For example:
   * name: bv
   * value: basketball-victoria
   */
  tenantSlugs?: Maybe<Array<TenantField>>;
};

export type ExternalAccountLinkingWithTenant = {
  __typename?: 'ExternalAccountLinkingWithTenant';
  config?: Maybe<ExternalAccountLinking>;
  tenantSlug?: Maybe<Scalars['String']>;
}

__typename?: 'ExternalAccountLinking';
  /** Allow the participant to link an external account with a different email to their PlayHQ email */
  allowDifferentEmailToPlayHQEmail?: Maybe<Scalars['Boolean']>;
  /** Should we allow the participant unlink their external account themselves */
  allowParticipantToUnlink?: Maybe<Scalars['Boolean']>;
  /** The URL of the OIDC/OAuth2 provider */
  authUri?: Maybe<Scalars['String']>;
  /** Layup application identifier as registered with the OIDC/OAuth2 provider */
  clientID?: Maybe<Scalars['String']>;
  /** The display friendly name, eg CricketiD */
  displayName?: Maybe<Scalars['String']>;
  /**
   * If external account linking is enabled, the FE should show the linking tile during
   * the registration flow
   */
  enabled: Scalars['Boolean'];
  /** The homepage for the external linking, eg https://id.cricket.com.au */
  externalURL?: Maybe<Scalars['String']>;
  /** URL pointing to an image that is the logo for the external account linking. EG the AFLID logo */
  logoURL?: Maybe<Scalars['String']>;
  /** The description/text used on the profile page to explain to the user how the linking works for the tenant */
  profilePageInfoText?: Maybe<Scalars['String']>;
  /** The layup redirect URI to receive a response from the OIDC/OAuth2 provider */
  redirectUri?: Maybe<Scalars['String']>;
  /**
   * In the registration flow, when the user signs in with an external account,
   * should we attempt to link the accounts for SSO as well.
   */
  shouldLinkSSOInRegistrationFlow?: Maybe<Scalars['Boolean']>;
  /** In the registration flow, should we show the tenant specific login page. For example show their button above ours. */
  showTenantSpecificLoginPageInRegistrationFlow?: Maybe<Scalars['Boolean']>;
  /** Markdown to be displayed on the tenant specific login page */
  tenantSpecificLoginPageMarkdown?: Maybe<Scalars['String']>;
};

export type MerchandiseFee = {
  __typename?: 'MerchandiseFee';
  amount: Price;
  /**
   * Category pairs returned null for registration related merchandise fees
   *
   * The nullable set of category/attribute pairs that define the given variant product.
   * For example, given a product that has the 'Size' and 'Colour' categories,
   * this variant product may be defined as a 'Small Red Shirt', or a 'Large Green
   * Shirt'.
   *
   * Unlike ProductVariantPair which provide all available categories in ProductVariant, this field
   * only returns selected categories that are relevant to the item in the cart.
   */
  categoryPairs?: Maybe<Array<CategoryPair>>;
  customFieldAnswers?: Maybe<Array<MerchandiseFeeCustomFieldResponse>>;
  description?: Maybe<Scalars['String']>;
  fulfilmentMethod: FulfilmentMethod;
  fulfilmentProvider?: Maybe<Scalars['String']>;
  /** Images returned null for registration related merchandise fees */
  images?: Maybe<Array<Image>>;
  organisation: DiscoverOrganisation;
  productID: Scalars['ID'];
  productType: ProductType;
  productVariantID: Scalars['ID'];
  quantity: Scalars['Int'];
}

__typename?: 'CategoryPair';
  id: Scalars['ID'];

__typename?: 'UpcomingTeamEventTimeline';
  /**
   * Events have occurred recently (no more than 1 day ago), and events that are upcoming next
   * week are found here. Most events will be allocated games of any status and some byes.
   * Byes are represented as `DiscoverRound`.
   *
   * Bookmarked entries that would result in duplicated entries are removed. Duplication is
   * determined by the type of event and the team. For example, if a user follows two teams
   * that would play against one another, the game would be duplicated.
   * Byes act differently as their identity is compounded by their round ID and the team.
   * If the user follows multiple teams that share a bye (i.e., these teams are having byes
   * on the same round), a record for each team will be given.
   */
  recentAndNextWeekEvents: Array<UpcomingTeamEvent>;
  /**
   * Upcoming events outside the week range specified above will reside in this type. Every
   * bookmarked team should have one element in this list. Games may be allocated or unallocated.
   * View the `UpcomingTeamEventItem` union type documentation for more details.
   */
  upcomingEvents: Array<UpcomingTeamEvent>;
};

export type Mutation = {
  __typename?: 'Mutation';
  accountConfirm: AccountConfirmation;
  accountUpdate: Account;
  addressUpdate: Address;
  checkoutSessionCreate: CheckoutSession;
  childSafetyUpdate?: Maybe<FieldSet>;
  childSafetyUpsert: ChildSafetyUpsertResponse;
  claimVerify: ProfileMerge;
  coachingAccreditationUpdate: CoachingAccreditation;
  /** Team manager reviews and confirms incident clearance */
  confirmIncidentClearance?: Maybe<Incident>;
  /** Unsubscribes an email from notifications for a tenant */
  emailNotificationUnsubscribe: EmailNotificationUnsubscribe;
  emergencyContactUpdate?: Maybe<EmergencyContact>;
  /**
   * Update game availability status for a participant. Participants generally do not have access to full game and team information
   * due to privacy reasons, so the response fields should be public facing (besides participant details)
   */
  gameAvailabilityUpdate?: Maybe<GameAvailabilityUpdateResponse>;
  /** Flag the game webhook as confirmed by the external source (such as a referee). */
  gameManageConfirmResults?: Maybe<Scalars['Boolean']>;
  /**
   * Pass in a signed base64-encoded token from an integration partner (such as
   * Refbook), and if valid return a long-lived JWT auth token with scoped manage
   * access, as well as the gameID from the token.
   */
  gameManageJWTGenerate?: Maybe<GameManageJwtGenerateResponse>;
  gameSheetGenerate?: Maybe<GameSheetGenerateResponse>;
  /** Update club award votes for players in a team in a game */
  gameTeamAwardVotesUpdate?: Maybe<GameTeamAward>;
  guardianCreate: Guardian;
  guardianDelete: Guardian;
  guardianUpdate: Guardian;
  /**
   * Create an identity verification session to receive a return URL for the user to complete the identity verification process
   * This method is used in the registration flow and requires participant id to be provided
   */
  identityVerificationSessionCreate?: Maybe<Scalars['String']>;
  /** Creates an incident */
  incidentCreate?: Maybe<Incident>;
  /** Deletes an incident */
  incidentDelete?: Maybe<Incident>;
  /** Updates an incident */
  incidentUpdate?: Maybe<Incident>;
  invoiceDownload?: Maybe<Document>;
  linkExternalAccount: ExternalAccount;
  /**
   * Migration operations - only available when MIGRATION_OPERATIONS_ENABLED=true
   * This is a separate operation as we do not allow creation of profiles like this under normal circumstances.
   */
  migrationProfileUpsert: Profile;
  myTeamsGameFillInPlayerUpdate?: Maybe<MyTeamsGameUpdateResponse>;
  myTeamsGamePaymentRequestCreate?: Maybe<MyTeamsGamePaymentRequestCreateResponse>;
  myTeamsGamePlayerUpdate?: Maybe<MyTeamsGameUpdateResponse>;
  myTeamsGameTeamUpdate?: Maybe<MyTeamsGameUpdateResponse>;
  myTeamsGameUpdate?: Maybe<MyTeamsGameUpdateResponse>;
  /**
   * For Gr4vy embed, transactions are authorized and not captured by their embedded form before
   * orderSubmit is called. At the point they are authorized we have the ability to set an external
   * identifier which we want to be the order ID, so we need to generate one.
   * It will be linked to the user that creates it for authorization purposes.
   */
  orderIdentifierGenerate: Scalars['String'];
  /**
   * Submits an order and charges the account specified by the token from the input arguments.
   * This mutation is a common for shop and registration orders, and to distinguish between the two
   * we use orderPurchaseScope.purchaseScope to determine the order type.
   */
  orderSubmit: Order;
  participantRegister?: Maybe<Participant>;
  permitRequestCreate?: Maybe<Permit>;
  postEmailUnsubscribe: PostEmailUnsubscribe;
  productsUpdateCart: Cart;
  productUpdateSocialTeamCart: Cart;
  profileClaim: ProfileMerge;
  profileEmailChange?: Maybe<Scalars['ID']>;
  profileEmailVerify?: Maybe<ProfileEmailChangeResult>;
  profileQuestionsUpdate?: Maybe<FieldSet>;
  profileUpdate?: Maybe<Profile>;
  registerPushNotificationTarget: PushNotificationTarget;
  savePushNotificationUserSettings: PushNotificationUserSettings;
  selfInitiatedIdentityVerificationSessionCreate?: Maybe<Scalars['String']>;
  /** If input contains an ID, it will update the existing cart, otherwise it will create a new cart. */
  shopCartUpsert?: Maybe<ShopCart>;
  socialTeamRegistrationSubmit: DiscoverTeam;
  /** Submits incident clearance */
  submitIncidentClearance?: Maybe<Incident>;
  transferRequestCreate: TransferRequest;
  unlinkExternalAccount: ExternalAccount;
  unregisterPushNotificationTarget?: Maybe<Scalars['String']>;
  updatePendingParticipant?: Maybe<Scalars['Boolean']>;
  /**
   * Generate a verification code to be used for claim verification. An email
   * or SMS message will be sent to the designated individual who can authorise
   * the claim. This can be used in a registration or self initiated flow.
   *
   * Determining whether a claim is valid uses the same approach as the
   * `Profile.duplicateProfiles` field resolver. Users can provide overrides that
   * allow users to find profiles that do not match previously set values.
   *
   * Please view the documentation in the `ClaimProfileInput` regarding the intents
   * which can be captured by this mutation.
   */
  verificationCodeGenerate: ProfileMerge;
  wwcUpdate: Wwc;
}

export const GameViewGameTeamStatisticsFragmentFragmentDoc = gql`
    fragment GameViewGameTeamStatisticsFragment on DiscoverGameTeamStatistics {
  players {
    playerNumber
    player {
      ... on DiscoverParticipant {
        id
        profile {
          id
          firstName
          lastName
        }

__typename?: 'Query';\n  account?: Maybe<Account>;\n  activityPaginated?: Maybe<ActivityPaginated>;\n  /** @deprecated Use place instead */\n  address?: Maybe<AddressInfo>;\n  availablePushNotificationTypes: Array<PushNotificationTypeDetails>;\n  /**\n   * Returns a non nullable list of nullable bookmarkable union types.\n   * The order of these bookmarks align with the `items` input given.\n   * If an element of the `codes` is malformed, the index of the\n   * response will be null and can be ignored.\n   *\n   * The type prefix should align with a GraphQL type, the ID and the\n   * tenant slug. This query can only support one tenant at a time.\n   * If `codes` contains bookmarks across multiple tenants it will\n   * be treated as a bad request. If the tenant header is provided,\n   * and the input entries do not define their own `tenant` field,\n   * the tenant defined in the header will implicitly be used.\n   *\n   * When profile bookmark inputs are provided, it is possible that\n   * the `DiscoverProfile` response will return `null`.
